# Compliance Evidence Bundle: SSO Settings Feature in Grafana

## Scenario

For a SOC 2 audit, your security team needs a compliance evidence bundle proving
that Grafana's SSO (Single Sign-On) settings control is implemented end-to-end.
You need to trace the `ssoSettingsApi` feature flag from its definition through
the SSO settings infrastructure, API endpoints, OAuth connector wiring, and
authentication registration to show the control is properly gated and enforced.

## Your Task

Find ALL files in `grafana/grafana` that form the SSO settings control across
these 4 layers:

### 1. Feature Flag Definition
- The feature flag registry where `ssoSettingsApi` is defined
- Generated constants files (Go, TypeScript) that reference this flag

### 2. SSO Settings Infrastructure
- The `Service` interface definition for SSO settings management
- The `Reloadable` interface for live configuration reloading
- The `SSOSettings` data model/struct with persistence annotations
- The `SSOSettingsStore` database layer for SSO setting persistence

### 3. API & Authentication Wiring
- The REST API endpoint registration (`/api/v1/sso-settings`) with access control middleware
- The `SocialService` provider that loads OAuth connectors when the flag is enabled
- The authentication client registration that conditionally enables LDAP based on the flag

### 4. Access Control & DI Registration
- The access control evaluators (`EvalAuthenticationSettings`, `OauthSettingsEvaluator`) that gate SSO admin UI access
- The `ProvideService` dependency injection function that wires the SSO settings store, API, fallback strategies, and reloadables

## Available Resources

Your ecosystem includes the following repositories:
- `grafana/grafana` at v11.4.0
- `grafana/loki` at v3.3.4

## Output Format

Create a file at `/workspace/answer.json` with your findings:

```json
{
  "files": [
    {"repo": "grafana/grafana", "path": "pkg/services/featuremgmt/registry.go"}
  ],
  "text": "Comprehensive explanation of how the 4 layers connect: feature flag definition → SSO settings infrastructure → API & authentication wiring → access control & DI registration."
}
```

**Important**: Use `grafana/grafana` as the exact `repo` identifier. Strip the
`github.com/` prefix that Sourcegraph MCP tools return.

**Deep Search hint**: This task requires synthesizing across feature management,
SSO settings infrastructure, OAuth connectors, and authentication registration
layers. Deep Search is particularly well-suited for tracing these cross-cutting
concerns.

## Evaluation

Your answer will be scored on:
- **File recall and precision**: Did you find the architecturally significant files across all 4 layers?
- **Keyword coverage**: Does your answer reference the key interfaces and types (`ssoSettingsApi`, `FlagSsoSettingsApi`, `SSOSettings`, `Reloadable`, `SSOSettingsStore`)?
- **Provenance**: Does your answer cite the correct repos and directory paths?
- **Rubric judge**: An LLM judge will assess evidence completeness, cross-component tracing, auditor actionability, and technical accuracy.

## Summary

The **`ssoSettingsApi`** feature flag is implemented end-to-end across these architecturally significant files:

### **Layer 1: Feature Flag Definition**
- `pkg/services/featuremgmt/toggles_gen.go` - Generated constants for `FlagSsoSettingsApi`, `FlagSsoSettingsLDAP`, `FlagSsoSettingsSAML`

### **Layer 2: SSO Settings Infrastructure**  
- `pkg/services/ssosettings/ssosettings.go` - Core interfaces (`Service`, `Reloadable`, `Store`, `FallbackStrategy`)
- `pkg/services/ssosettings/models/models.go` - `SSOSettings` struct with xorm persistence annotations (table: `sso_setting`)
- `pkg/services/ssosettings/database/database.go` - `SSOSettingsStore` database layer implementation
- `pkg/services/ssosettings/strategies/` - Fallback strategies for OAuth, LDAP, SAML (backwards compatibility)

### **Layer 3: API & Authentication Wiring**
- `pkg/services/ssosettings/api/api.go` - REST API endpoints at `/api/v1/sso-settings` with access control middleware
- `pkg/services/ssosettings/ssosettingsimpl/service.go` - **Critical gating**: `if features.IsEnabledGlobally(FlagSsoSettingsApi) { registerAPIEndpoints() }` (line 94-96)
- `pkg/services/authn/authnimpl/registration.go` - **Conditional LDAP registration**: `ssoSettingsLDAP := FlagSsoSettingsApi && FlagSsoSettingsLDAP` (line 56-61)
- `pkg/services/authn/clients/oauth.go` and `ldap.go` - OAuth and LDAP authentication clients

### **Layer 4: Access Control & DI Registration**
- `pkg/services/accesscontrol/roles.go` - Permission actions (`ActionSettingsRead`/`Write`) and scopes
- `pkg/services/ssosettings/ssosettingsimpl/service.go` - ProvideService dependency inj

Get, List, Upsert, Delete operations with soft-delete support\\n  - Filters by `is_deleted` column for logical deletion\\n\\n**Fallback Strategies** (`pkg/services/ssosettings/strategies/`):\\n- **OAuthStrategy**: Loads OAuth provider configs from cfg.SSOSettingsConfigurableProviders and legacy OAuth config settings\\n- **LDAPStrategy**: Loads LDAP config from cfg.LDAP* settings for backwards compatibility\\n- **SAMLStrategy**: Loads SAML settings from licensed provider config\\n\\nThese strategies enable the system to function with both legacy (file-based) and new (database-backed) SSO configurations simultaneously.\\n\\n### Layer 3: API & Authentication Wiring\\n\\n**REST API Endpoints** (`pkg/services/ssosettings/api/api.go`):\\n- **Route**: `/api/v1/sso-settings`\\n- **Endpoints**:\\n  - `GET /` - List all SSO settings with redacted secrets (requires `ActionSettingsRead`)\\n  - `GET /:key` - Get SSO settings for a provider (requires `ActionSettingsRead` with provider scope)\\n  - `PUT /:key` - Update/upsert SSO settings (requires `ActionSettingsWrite` with provider scope)\\n  - `DELETE /:key` - Delete SSO settings (soft delete, requires `ActionSettingsWrite` with provider scope)\\n- All endpoints are protected with access control middleware using:\\n  - `ac.EvalPermission(ac.ActionSettingsRead/Write, ac.ScopeSettingsOAuth(key))` evaluators\\n  - Access checks filter settings by provider scope\\n\\n**Feature Flag Gating** (`pkg/services/ssosettings/ssosettingsimpl/service.go`):\\n- **Critical Control Point** (lines 94-96):\\n  ```go\\n  if features.IsEnabledGlobally(featuremgmt.FlagSsoSettingsApi) {\\n    ssoSettingsApi := api.ProvideApi(svc, routeRegister, ac)\\n    ssoSettingsApi.RegisterAPIEndpoints()\\n  }\\n  ```\\n  The entire REST API endpoint registration is **gated by FlagSsoSettingsApi**. When the flag is disabled, the `/api/v1/sso-settings` endpoints are not registered at all.\\n\\n**Conditional Provider Support** (same file, lines 63-75):\\n- LDAP provider is added to the providers list when `FlagSsoSettingsLDAP` is enabled\\n- SAML provider is added when licensed and `FlagSsoSettingsSAML` is enabled\\n- These control which providers appear in the SSO settings API responses\\n\\n**Fallback Strategies Wiring** (lines 51-54):\\n- OAuth, LDAP (conditional), and SAML (conditional) fallback strategies are registered\\n- These enable loading settings from legacy config sources when not yet migrated to database\\n\\n**Authentication Client Registration** (`pkg/services/authn/authnimpl/registration.go`):\\n- **LDAP Client Conditional Registration** (lines 56-61):\\n  ```go\\n  ssoSettingsLDAP := features.IsEnabledGlobally(featuremgmt.FlagSsoSettingsApi) && \\n                     features.IsEnabledGlobally(featuremgmt.FlagSsoSettingsLDAP)\\n  if cfg.LDAPAuthEnabled || ssoSettingsLDAP {\\n    ldap := clients.ProvideLDAP(cfg, ldapService, userService, authInfoService)\\n    proxyClients = append(proxyClients, ldap)\\n    passwordClients = append(passwordClients, ldap)\\n  }\\n  ```\\n  LDAP authentication is registered when either legacy LDAP is enabled OR both SSO settings API and LDAP feature flags are enabled.\\n\\n- **OAuth Client Auto-Registration** (lines 98-101):\\n  ```go\\n  for name := range socialService.GetOAuthProviders() {\\n    clientName := authn.ClientWithPrefix(name)\\n    authnSvc.RegisterClient(clients.ProvideOAuth(clientName, cfg, oauthTokenService, \\n                            socialService, settingsProviderService, features))\\n  }\\n  ```\\n  OAuth clients are auto-registered for all providers. The OAuth client internally loads provider configuration from `socialService.GetOAuthInfoProvider()`, which pulls from SSO settings when FlagSsoSettingsApi is enabled.\\n\\n### Layer 4: Access Control & DI Registration\\n\\n**Permission Actions** (`pkg/services/accesscontrol/roles.go`):\\n- **ActionSettingsRead**: Used to grant read access to SSO settings\\n- **ActionSettingsWrite**: Used to grant write access to SSO settings\\n- **ScopeSettingsOAuth(key)**: Scoped access to specific OAuth provider settings\\n\\n**Role Definitions** (same file):\\n- **SettingsReaderRole** (fixed:settings:reader):\\n  - Grants `ActionSettingsRead` with `ScopeSettingsAll`\\n  - Applied to admin UI for viewing SSO configurations\\n\\n**Complete Dependency Injection** (`pkg/services/ssosettings/ssosettingsimpl/service.go`):\\nThe ProvideService function orchestrates the entire system:\\n1. Creates SSOSettingsStore (database persistence)\\n2. Registers fallback strategies for legacy config compatibility\\n3. Conditionally adds LDAP and SAML to supported providers based on feature flags\\n4. **Conditionally registers REST API** when FlagSsoSettingsApi is enabled\\n5. Wires secrets service for encryption/decryption\\n6. Registers metrics and usage stats collection\\n\\n## Evidence Chain for Compliance Audits\\n\\nThis architecture demonstrates complete control-flow gating:\\n\\n1. **Feature Flag Enforcement**: FlagSsoSettingsApi must be explicitly enabled for the API to be registered\\n2. **API Protection**: All endpoints require access control evaluation with specific OAuth permissions\\n3. **Authentication Client Gating**: LDAP registration depends on both FlagSsoSettingsApi and FlagSsoSettingsLDAP\\n4. **Database Persistence**: SSO settings are stored in the `sso_setting` table with audit timestamps (created, updated)\\n5. **Fallback Strategy**: Legacy config sources are supported but can be migrated to database-backed settings\\n6. **Live Reloading**: Reloadable interface allows providers to validate and reload settings when changed via API\\n\\nThe control is enforced at multiple levels: feature flag registration, API endpoint registration, authentication client registration, and permission evaluation. Disabling FlagSsoSettingsApi effectively disables the entire SSO settings management capability while preserving legacy authentication mechanisms.\"\n}\n",
